 Religious importance of Nainital: In the Manas section of Skanda Purana it has been called 'tri-rishi-sarovar'
 ye teen rishi atri, pulsthya or pulaha rishi the
 When they could not find any water in this area, they made a big pit here and filled the holy water of Mansarovar in it
 usee sarovar ko aaj naini taal ke rup main janaa jaataa he
 It is believed that the importance of taking a dip in Naini Tal is as sacred as taking a dip in Mansarovar
 iske alaava nainital ko 64 shakti peethon main se ek mana jaataa he
 It is believed that when Lord Shiva was wandering all over the universe with the body of Mother Sati, the eyes of Mother (nain) fell here
 mata kii aakhen yahaan giri thi isliye is jagah kaa naam naini taal padaa

 rukne kii vyavastha kahaan ho

 ye kahani he ek bhakt or bhagwaan kii, jahaan bhakt kii bhakthi or aasthaa ke kaaran bhakt ke saath hameshaa ke liye jud gaya bhagwaan kaa naam

 Located in the remote village of Chinchwad
 chinchvaad janmasthali he ek aise sant kii jisaki bhakthi or aasthaa ne likh di ek aisi kahani, jiske baad unke naam ke saath hi jud gaya ganpati kaa bhi naam
 There was a saint in the fifteenth century, named Morya Gosavi
 kehete hai bhagwaan ganesh ke aashirwad se hi morya gosaavi kaa janm hua tha or morya gosaavi bhi apane mata-pita kii tarah bhagwaan ganesh kii puja aradhana karte the
 Every year on the auspicious occasion of Ganesh Chaturthi, Morya used to walk from Chinchwad to worship Morgaon Ganesh
 kaha jaataa he ki badhati umr kii vajah se ek din khud bhagwaan ganesh unke sapane main aae or unase kaha ki unki murti unhen nadi main milegi

 The jayakara that started from Chinchwad village near Pune is on the tongue of every devotee of Ganapati Bappa today
 lekin jahaan tak ganpati puja ke saarvajanik aayojan kaa sawaal he to isaki shuruyaat svantratata senaanee balgangadhar lokmaanya tilak ne kii thi
